name:A‚ÄçR‚ÄçC‚Äç5‚Äç5‚Äç5‚Äç5
info:Deluxe Double Room
info:Stayed in April 2024
info:Couples
info:7 Reviews
rating:4.2
posted:Posted May 5, 2024
msg:The stay at the 4points by Sheraton Shenzhou Peninsula was very enjoyable. From Sanya Airport we took the HSR to Shenzhou station and ordered a Didi there to take us to the hotel (~20min). Apparently there is also an Airport shuttle service by the hotel but to my knowledge it isnt free and only goes 2 times a day. Anyways, once there, the check in was quick and convenient. The walk to the room at the east end was quite long (big hotel). The room was quite big, clean and had all necessary equipment, but it is noticeable that everything has come to an age or appeared to be worn out a little. Also the bathroom always smelled a bit ‚Äûsmokey‚Äú and there was also an noticeable smell from the toilet drainage. All in all the room was still satisfying yet it comes at a quite expensive price where you could expect better. The breakfast had many meal choices, but nothing that was over the top. Especially the very limited fruit offer on a tropical island like Hainan was disappointing. For a Trip-5 Star-hotel at this price point it could do better. 
The outside facilities of the hotel were very nice and relatively well maintained. The big pool was a highlight. Also its location directly at the sea with a big beautiful beach is nice. But yet again the downside is you are not allowed to swim in the sea. Yet always someone was trying to sell some surfing courses, jetski ride or other activities. I understand the safety concern, but as an experienced swimmer with lifeguard training it was a bit ridiculous. Still having a long sunset walk at the beach is amazing. For having dinner, there are a few decent choices in the 1km footwalk vicinity. Some restaurant areas can be reached by walking down the beach. My favorite though was the ‚ÄûCorona-Bar‚Äú directly in front of the hotel, which serves semi-authentic Mexican dishes and nice cocktails. It comes at a higher price point, but if you make the correct food choices it is very delicious. 
Check out was also quick and comfortable and to summarize, we had an enjoyable stay. I only think for the price you pay there is still some space for little improvements by the hotel.
----------------------------------------

msg:The hotel is beautifully situated with its own beach. The landscaping and grounds are picturesque as are the ocean views. I have previously stayed in big hotels in Sanya that involve long walks to the facilities and the beach. However, this hotel is really nicely sized. The lagoon pools and infinity pools were great, though I did wonder a bit about the cleanliness levels. I was initially concerned about reviews saying the place looked aged, but in person the rooms seemed fine, spacious and clean. The service was excellent on every level. They did not have a business center but they helped me out with some business needs. The breakfast was diverse and they made sure to keep the buffet filled up despite a large number of diners. All in all, it was a very refreshing and enjoyable stay. Note that taking a train from Sanya Airport to Wanning is not difficult and economical if the timing works well for your flights.

msg:Hainan Wanning Sheraton Shenzhou Peninsula Resort Hotel 1
When traveling to Hainan in recent years, I always stayed away from the crowds of Sanya, and this trip to Hainan was no exception. After landing in Sanya, I immediately drove to the beautiful Wanning.
The Shenzhou Peninsula in Wanning is surrounded by the sea on three sides and is an hour and a half drive from Sanya. On this peninsula with an area of ‚Äã‚Äãonly 24 square kilometers, there are only three high-end five-star hotels. This time I chose to stay at the Sheraton Shenzhou Peninsula Resort in Wanning. Staying here can fully enjoy the sun, sea and beach and your own private time [Hotel Location Sheraton Shenzhou Peninsula Resort Hotel is adjacent to Wanning Shimei Bay. It only takes ten minutes to drive from Shimei Bay to Shenzhou Peninsula. The hotel is located in Shenzhou Letao Bay on the peninsula is hidden in a tropical garden with coconut breeze and sea charm. The hotel is close to the sea, and the 700-meter-long golden beach is right outside the door.
Coastline, there are nearly 50,000 square meters of golden beach, in the room
You can enjoy the beautiful endless sea view. [Hotel environment
